Please free up space."\n        exit 1\n    fi\n    print_success "Available disk space: ${DISK_SPACE}GB âœ“"\n}\n\n# Setup environment\nsetup_environment() {\n    print_step "Setting up environment..."\n    \n    # Create necessary directories\n    mkdir -p logs outputs models temp database\n    \n    # Copy environment file if not exists\n    if [ ! -f .env ]; then\n        if [ -f .env.example ]; then\n            cp .env.example .env\n            print_success "Created .env file from .env.example"\n        else\n            print_warning ".env.example not found. âœ“"\n    else\n        print_warning "Some services may still be starting..."\n        docker-compose -f docker-compose.ai.yml ps\n    fi\n}\n\n# Install Node Dependencies\ninstall_dependencies() {\n    print_step "Installing Node.js dependencies..."\n    \n    if [ ! -d "node_modules" ]; then\n        print_status "Installing dependencies for the first time..."\n        npm install\n    else\n        print_status "Checking for dependency updates..."\n        npm ci --silent || npm install\n    fi\n    print_success "Dependencies installed âœ“"\n}\n\n# Start Frontend\nstart_frontend() {\n    print_step "Starting JeanTrail Frontend..."\n    \n    # Kill existing processes\n    pkill -f "vite\\|npm run dev" 2>/dev/null || true\n    \n    # Start development server\n    print_status "Starting Vite development server..."\n    npm run dev > logs/frontend.log 2>&1 &\n    FRONTEND_PID=$!\n    \n    # Wait for frontend to start\n    sleep 10\n    \n    # Check if frontend is running\n    if curl -s http://localhost:1420 > /dev/null; then\n        print_success "Frontend is running on http://localhost:1420 âœ“"\n    else\n        print_error "Frontend failed to start. ğŸš€${NC}\\n"\n}\n\n# Error handling\nhandle_error() {\n    print_error "Something went wrong during startup."\n    print_status "Checking logs..."\n    echo -e "\\n${YELLOW}Docker logs:${NC}"\n    docker-compose -f docker-compose.ai.yml logs --tail=20\n    echo -e "\\n${YELLOW}Frontend logs:${NC}"\n    tail -20 logs/frontend.log 2>/dev/null || echo "No frontend logs found"\n    exit 1\n}\n\n# Trap errors\ntrap \'handle_error\' ERR\n\n# Main execution\nmain() {\n    echo -e "${PURPLE}ğŸš€ Starting JeanTrail OS...${NC}\\n"\n    \n    check_requirements\n    setup_environment\n    start_ai_services\n    install_dependencies\n    start_frontend\n    show_success\n    \n    # Keep script running\n    echo -e "${CYAN}Press Ctrl+C to stop all services...${NC}"\n    while true; do\n        sleep 5\n    done\n}\n\n# Handle Ctrl+C gracefully\ncleanup() {\n    echo -e "\\n${YELLOW}Shutting down JeanTrail OS...${NC}"\n    pkill -f "vite\\|npm run dev" 2>/dev/null || true\n    docker-compose -f docker-compose.ai.yml down\n    print_success "All services stopped. require(\'redis\');\nconst client = Redis.createClient({\n  url: process.env.REDIS_URL,\n  retryDelayOnFailover: 100,\n  maxRetriesPerRequest: 3\n});\n\n// Cache middleware\nconst cache = (duration = 300) => {\n  return async (req, res, next) => {\n    const key = `cache:${req.originalUrl}`;\n    const cached = await client.get(key);\n    \n    if (cached) {\n      return res.json(JSON.parse(cached));\n    }\n    \n    res.sendResponse = res.json;\n    res.json = (body) => {\n      client.setex(key, duration, JSON.stringify(body));\n      res.sendResponse(body);\n    };\n    \n    next();\n  };\n};\n```\n\n---\n\n## ğŸ”§ Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n#### 1. All APIs use JSON for request/response format and follow RESTful principles.\n\n### Base URLs\n- **Development**: `http://localhost:1420/api`\n- **Production**: `https://your-domain.com/api`\n- **AI Services**: `http://localhost:8001`\n\n### Common Headers\n```http\nContent-Type: application/json\nAuthorization: Bearer <JWT_TOKEN>\nX-API-Version: v1\n```\n\n### Response Format\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {},\n  "message": "Operation completed successfully",\n  "timestamp": "2024-12-09T15:30:00Z",\n  "requestId": "req_123456789"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## ğŸ” Authentication\n\n### JWT Authentication\nAll API endpoints (except public ones) require JWT authentication.\n\n#### Obtain JWT Token\n```http\nPOST /api/auth/login\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "email": "user@jeantrail.ai",\n  "password": "user_password"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9...",\n    "refreshToken": "refresh_token_here",\n    "expiresIn": 3600,\n    "user": {\n      "id": "user_123",\n      "email": "user@jeantrail.ai",\n      "role": "user"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Refresh Token\n```http\nPOST /api/auth/refresh\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "refreshToken": "refresh_token_here"\n}\n```\n\n#### Logout\n```http\nPOST /api/auth/logout\nAuthorization: Bearer <JWT_TOKEN>\n```\n\n---\n\n## ğŸ¤– AI Services APIs\n\n### Qwen-3 Text Generation\n\n#### Generate Text\n```http\nPOST /api/ai/qwen/generate\nAuthorization: Bearer <JWT_TOKEN>\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "prompt": "Hello, Jean! How can you help me today?",\n  "maxTokens": 2048,\n  "temperature": 0.7,\n  "topP": 0.9,\n  "stream": false,\n  "context": {\n    "userId": "user_123",\n    "sessionId": "session_456"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "text": "Hello! I\'m Jean, your AI assistant. I can help you with browsing, file management, and more!",\n    "usage": {\n      "promptTokens": 25,\n      "completionTokens": 30,\n      "totalTokens": 55\n    },\n    "model": "qwen-3-72b",\n    "finishReason": "stop"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Stream Text Generation\n```http\nPOST /api/ai/qwen/stream\nAuthorization: Bearer <JWT_TOKEN>\n```\n\n**Request Body:** Same as generate, with `"stream": true`\n\n**Response:** Server-Sent Events (SSE)\n```\ndata: {"type": "token", "value": "Hello"}\ndata: {"type": "token", "value": "! I\'m"}\ndata: {"type": "done", "usage": {...}}\n```\n\n### SDXL Image Generation\n\n#### Generate Image\n```http\nPOST /api/ai/sdxl/generate\nAuthorization: Bearer <JWT_TOKEN>\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "prompt": "A futuristic AI assistant in a digital landscape",\n  "negativePrompt": "blurry, low quality, distorted",\n  "width": 1024,\n  "height": 1024,\n  "steps": 30,\n  "guidanceScale": 7.5,\n  "seed": 42,\n  "style": "photorealistic"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "imageUrl": "https://api.jeantrail.ai/images/generated_123456.png",\n    "imageId": "img_123456",\n    "metadata": {\n      "prompt": "A futuristic AI assistant...",\n      "model": "sdxl-base-1.0",\n      "steps": 30,\n      "seed": 42,\n      "generationTime": 15.2\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Whisper Speech-to-Text\n\n#### Transcribe Audio\n```http\nPOST /api/ai/whisper/transcribe\nAuthorization: Bearer <JWT_TOKEN>\nContent-Type: multipart/form-data\n```\n\n**Request:**\n```\nfile: <audio_file>\nlanguage: "en" // optional\nmodel: "whisper-1"\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "text": "Hello Jean, can you help me browse the web?",\n    "language": "en",\n    "duration": 3.5,\n    "confidence": 0.95\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Coqui TTS (Text-to-Speech)\n\n#### Generate Speech\n```http\nPOST /api/ai/tts/generate\nAuthorization: Bearer <JWT_TOKEN>\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "text": "Hello! I\'m Jean, your AI assistant.",\n  "voice": "default",\n  "language": "en",\n  "speed": 1.0,\n  "format": "mp3"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "audioUrl": "https://api.jeantrail.ai/audio/speech_123456.mp3",\n    "audioId": "audio_123456",\n    "duration": 2.3,\n    "format": "mp3"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## ğŸ§  Jean Assistant APIs\n\n### Chat with Jean\n\n#### Send Message\n```http\nPOST /api/jean/chat\nAuthorization: Bearer <JWT_TOKEN>\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "message": "Help me find information about AI browsers",\n  "context": {\n    "currentUrl": "https://jeantrail.ai",\n    "activeTab": "search",\n    "userPreferences": {\n      "language": "en",\n      "timezone": "UTC"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "message": "I\'ll help you find information about AI browsers. Let me search for the latest developments...",\n    "actions": [\n      {\n        "type": "search",\n        "query": "AI browsers 2024",\n        "confidence": 0.95\n      },\n      {\n        "type": "open_tab",\n        "url": "https://example.com/ai-browsers",\n        "confidence": 0.87\n      }\n    ],\n    "sessionId": "session_456",\n    "messageId": "msg_789"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Execute Action\n```http\nPOST /api/jean/execute\nAuthorization: Bearer <JWT_TOKEN>\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "actionId": "action_123",\n  "confirm": true\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "executed": true,\n    "result": {\n      "type": "search_completed",\n      "results": [\n        {\n          "title": Joi.string().valid(\'development\', \'production\', \'test\').required(),\n  PORT: Joi.number().port().default(1420),\n  DATABASE_URL: Joi.string().uri().required(),\n  REDIS_URL: Joi.number().min(1).max(4096).default(2048)\n});\n\n// Validate configuration\nexport function validateConfig(): void {\n  const { error } = configSchema.validate(process.env);\n  if (error) {\n    throw new Error(`Configuration validation failed: ${error.message}`);\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## ğŸ“Š Configuration Examples\n\n### High-Performance Setup\n```bash\n# High-performance configuration\nNODE_ENV=production\nLOG_LEVEL=warn\n\n# Optimized database\nDB_POOL_SIZE=50\nDB_TIMEOUT=10000\n\n# AI optimizations\nJEAN_MAX_TOKENS=1024\nAI_TIMEOUT=60000\n\n# Performance features\nCOMPRESSION_ENABLED=true\nCACHE_ENABLED=true\nRATE_LIMIT_MAX=1000\n```\n\n### Privacy-Focused Setup\n```bash\n# Privacy-focused configuration\nPRIVACY_SHARE_STATS=false\nPRIVACY_TELEMETRY=false\nPRIVACY_CRASH_REPORTS=false\n\n# Security hardening\nJWT_EXPIRES_IN=1h\nRATE_LIMIT_MAX=50\nCORS_ORIGIN=https://your-domain.com\n\n# Data retention\nLOG_RETENTION_DAYS=7\nCACHE_TTL=300\nSESSION_TIMEOUT=1800\n```\n\n### Development Setup\n```bash\n# Development configuration\nNODE_ENV=development\nLOG_LEVEL=debug\n\n# Local } from \'events\';\n\nexport class ConfigManager extends EventEmitter {\n  private config: Map<string, any> = new Map();\n  \n  update(key: string, value: any): void {\n    this.config.set(key, value);\n    this.emit(\'config:updated\', { key, value });\n  }\n  \n  get(key: string): any {\n    return this.config.get(key);\n  }\n  \n  reload(): void {\n    // Reload configuration from environment\n    this.emit(\'config:reloaded\');\n  }\n}\n\n// Usage example\nconst configManager = new ConfigManager();\nconfigManager.on(\'config:updated\', ({ key, value }) => {\n  console.log(`Configuration updated: ${key} = ${value}`);\n});\n```\n\n---\n\n## ğŸ“‹ Configuration Checklist\n\n### Pre-deployment Checklist\n- [ ] Environment variables set correctly\n- [ ] Database Restart affected services\ndocker-compose restart\n```\n\n---\n\n## ğŸ”¬ Advanced Debugging\n\n### Enable Debug Logging\n```bash\n# Set debug level\nexport LOG_LEVEL=debug\nexport Profiling\n```bash\n# Profile Node.js\nnpm run build -- --profile\nnode --inspect dist/index.js\n\n# Profile Docker containers\ndocker exec jeantrail_qwen-3-72b_1 py-spy top --pid 1\n\n# Memory profiling\nnode --inspect --heap-prof dist/index.js\n```\n\n### Network Debugging\n```bash\n# Check network connections\nnetstat -tulpn | grep :1420\n\n# Monitor network traffic\ntcpdump -i any port 1420\n\n# Test latency\ncurl -w "@curl-format.txt" http://localhost:1420\n```\n\n### Database Debugging\n```bash\n# Monitor PostgreSQL queries\ndocker exec jeantrail_postgres_1 psql -U jeantrail -c "\nSELECT query, calls, total_time, mean_time \nFROM pg_stat_statements \nORDER BY total_time DESC \nLIMIT 10;"\n\n# Check database locks\ndocker exec jeantrail_postgres_1 psql -U jeantrail -c "\nSELECT blocked_locks.pid AS blocked_pid,\n       blocked_activity.usename AS blocked_user,\n       blocking_locks.pid AS blocking_pid,\n       blocking_activity.usename AS blocking_user,\n       blocked_activity.query AS blocked_statement,\n       blocking_activity.query AS current_statement_in_blocking_process\nFROM pg_catalog.pg_locks blocked_locks\nJOIN pg_catalog.pg_stat_activity blocked_activity ON blocked_activity.pid = blocked_locks.pid\nJOIN pg_catalog.pg_locks blocking_locks ON blocking_locks.locktype = blocked_locks.locktype\nJOIN pg_catalog.pg_stat_activity blocking_activity ON blocking_activity.pid = blocking_locks.pid\nWHERE NOT blocked_locks.granted;"\n```\n\n---\n\n## ğŸ“Š Monitoring & Diagnostics\n\n### Real-time Monitoring\n```bash\n# System monitoring\nfor port in 8001 8002 8003 8004; do\n    echo "Port $port:"\n    curl -s http://localhost:$port/health || echo "DOWN"\n    echo "---"\ndone\n```\n\n### Log Analysis\n```bash\n# Search for jeantrail < backup.sql\n\n# Reset database\ndocker exec jeantrail_postgres_1 psql -U jeantrail -c "DROP SCHEMA public CASCADE; CREATE SCHEMA public;"\ndocker exec jeantrail_postgres_1 psql -U
